Dimitri's Postal Place is a private business. Some people use his business as a post office to drop off their boxes for mailing.  Dimitri provides free mailing to his customers, as a courtesy, with the exception of UPS, which he now charges $1 for most box sizes. PARKING

I have tried finding parking for over 15 mins before, they are always jam busy packed in this parking lot. I dislike this! There are additional parking behind the building and yes there are usually one or 2 slots open. i would recommend you just jog or run or walk or bike if you live nearby. Otherwise be prepare to stress over parking

INTERIOR

Inside is alway busy. I think the slowest time is usually is the mid afternoon like one ish to 3 ish. Also inside is crowded with lots of machines in the cardio and weight room as well. Also sometimes really warm and smell of sweat is what you can smell.

MACHINES

They did have old cardio machines but lately they did some upgrade and got some new machines so this boosts the place for a additional star. They are usually wet and dirty after someones workout who don't wipe after themselves like todays treadmill i got on. I usually try not to touch the machines and if i do i will go wash hands asap.

WEIGHT ROOM

They are a bit more organized for the weights re racking. Sometimes it could be messy and in the wrong category while people mis re rack them. The weight room is small and i feel like everyone is looking at each other lol.

STAFFS

The employees here are usually friendly and helpful. They are nice and always greet you when you walk in or walk out. They help change channels or help you operate a machine if help is needed.

VIBE

The vibe in here i feel like its chill place. Also feel like i workout with lots of elder people since this gym is more elder people attend during day time. Sometimes i feel like the elders are way more healthy and in shape for me by always going and seeing them go at it lol. i feel like everyone who goes here are to workout and stay healthy and are friendly.

LOCKERS

The lockers are old and usually you will need to bring your own lock to lock your stuff. Also they have an open shower room with no privacy. The stalls are usually wet and humid from the steam from the shower rooms.

SAUANA AND STEAM ROOM AND JACUZZI

Love the steam room, i feel like i demo everything from my body after a good steam after my workout. It also relaxes all my muscles and aches and pains from the body. Also feels like i did a deep cleanse on my face like a facial dextox. It is wet inside and adding your sweat can make you drench when you walk out.

The sauna is a dry version of a steam room. This one is more popular than the steam room, because no one wants to be drenched wet and go into the car or back into the gym. Also i feel like this helps you dry off from the steam room. also love how you go in dry and come out with real sweat dripping from your face.

TO SUM IT UP

I love the location which is in a nice area. I also love how it is close to my home. Love how My goal of coming here to get a good quality workout and be done with my workout asap and get out of there. Also love how there is a starbucks like 2 min walk and get a ice cold drink after. Thanks for reading and have a good workout and day lol.< /Text>

<Text>The food here is a little bit on the pricey side but is still quite filling. The burgers were quite greasy but remained on the gourmet side. I ordered the mushroom and swiss burger with a side of fries. When I got my dish, I was presented with the beef patty, lettuce, onions, pickles, tomatoes, and the bread all separate, requiring me to have to assemble my own burger. This was a first for me but wasn't an issue in any way. The water here tasted a little bit strange but wasn't bad enough where I wouldn't drink it. The food itself was delicious and I received a generous amount of mushroom and swiss. Food wise, this establishment gets a 4/5.

The service here was not awful, but my friend did notice that our waiter had a cut on his forearm with blood visible. It did make us a bit uncomfortable as the waiter did use his forearms to balance our plates when serving us, so this could be seen as a bit unsanitary. Despite all of this, the server was nice and accommodating.

All in all, you might have a better experience elsewhere, but if you're craving some greasy gourmet burgers, this is the place to be.</Text>< pictures>

I would rate this place 0 stars if I could. I tried to type my whole horror story here, but apparently Google has a word limit. This place has the worst communication, and lacks all basic notions of human decency. They no compassion, understanding or empathy skills. They will have you go in for appointments just to waste your time and bill your insurance provider for it. If you ever had the misfortune of coming here, its probably because you're on Denti-Cal. They love to take advantage of being a Denti-Cal provider. If you're on Denti-Cal, they will view you as a money bag. They took x-rays even when they weren't needed, as I had some I could've sent them from my last dentist. They had me show up for surgery one day just to tell me that my tooth was too close to the nerve, so they needed to file for sedation approval with Denti-Cal. Appointment fee they just exploited from Denti-Cal right there.This is a conclusion even Patrick Star could've come to just by looking at the x-ray. When I finally did go for my wisdom teeth removal surgery 5 months later after first seeing them, it was one of the worst days of my life. they gave me two days notice to find. a driver who could stay on the premises during my surgery, and when I wet in and tried to explain to them I could make that happen, the receptionist says no you need a driver or this isn't happening today. I tell her we are in a effing pandemic and you guys only gave me two days notice to find a driver who could STAY. Her attitude falls to the floor, and then has the audacity to say "It's always something with you every time you come here, isn't it?" I respond by saying well maybe it's because your customer service as a business is sub-prime and there's always a reason to complain about something at this god-foresaken place. She hands me forms to sign, and says that they won't do it unless the driver stays. My driver says its fine, he can stay in his car and use his wifi hotspot, since the clinic refused to offer him wifi to do his work with. All Western Dental sees its customers as is a money bag. They lack any basic customer service skills. When I couldn't stop crying, they forced me into a wheelchair and shoved me into my roommates car. I will never go back to this place. It would have saved me 2.5 hours of being poorly treated while patiently waiting for a teeth cleaning from the moment I entered (Yelper Eddy P is right, the front office staff do act like you're an inconvenience and so does everyone else, including the dentist I had. The only exception was Mandy, a really kind X-Ray technician I am sorry wasn't on the list in the website on the paper she gave me for a review about her service, I was going to give her a positive one in the context of the bad experience, she keeps the humanity of that place alive).

Anyway, back to the rest of the experience which makes me recommend you steer clear. While waiting, I was sent to use a bathroom that had a blood stain in it right in front of the toilet (yes, this actually happened), and when I finally got to the dentist got sighed at when I asked to add a mouth guard to my teeth cleaning and the dentist told me he would be "right back"...

At this time, it had been almost 1.25 hours of just waiting to see him, which hey, I understand, everyone gets busy.

BUT after he said he'd be back... another hour went by and still no dentist. So I asked someone I saw if they could please update me about when I would be seen.

Then, without explanation, a woman came over and, without saying anything about my dentist, told me my mouth guard and cleaning would be $490. I asked her why and she just repeated it and deducted other things to make it less expensive. She seemed surprised when I told her I had insurance. And was unapologetic about having not added or even checked for my insurance.

She then abruptly said it was an ortho surgery day and she had just gotten back from lunch, so I needed to understand. What I understood from her tone is that I was an inconvenience to her. But patiently still I told her I was frustrated with my poor treatment but thanked her for her help.

Then when it was time to pay the recalculated insurance price, she told me I couldn't get my treatments unless I had the physical FSA card I share with my husband even though they had all of his insurance info (we share the same plan) and I had pictures of the card as well as my ID and all other proof needed. This is not the upsetting part because it was only $98. What was upsetting is she told me, now 2.5 hours after arriving, that I would need to reschedule my teeth cleaning and mouth guard appointments.

I told her I wanted to speak to the manager and this is when it truly got ugly. She just said ok and took off, leaving me to wonder if I should follow so I just kind of walked behind her not knowing what to do when at least two other employees watched me and gave me stare downs. This was insult to injury because all I wanted were the simple services I'd come in for.

When told unapologetically the manager wasn't there and that maybe I could leave my number to have her call, at which point it did not seem a sincere gesture, I said I'd wait. I felt absolutely shunned at this point and like a nuisance for simply trying to be heard about what happened. Like my being frustrated was not unacceptable.

So after sitting in the waiting room quietly but feeling tension escalate and deciding I deserved better than that toxicity, I left with the manager's card (after going back up and asking, they did not offer to provide me with it).

I decided that surely this poor of treatment must stem from the top and not to push my luck. So here I am on Google Reviews trying to save others from this experience.

I'm truly sorry if you have an HMO where this is your only option. I felt physically put at risk (blood in the bathroom??) and shut down for having needs -- isn't dentistry still customer service? I have a PPO and will be going elsewhere. If you can, I advise you steer clear, too.< /review><pics>None<//pics>< resp>

If I could give them 0 Stars I would. It was horrible!!! My family and I, went to Western Dental to receive services with dental care on 10/17/2014.  He went to the office and found out he had multiple cavities and needed a root canal. He had his teeth cleaned and fluoride treatment applied. WD then looked up his credit to see if he would qualify for a dental contract. He said that he didn't want the contract until he talked to me. Stacy Bedolla put through the contract and started the payment plan without his consent or his signature. When I went to the office later that day to have my two daughter's teeth cleaned and looked at, Western Dental had cancelled our appointments without calling us without telling. Then they tried to accommodate us with almost a 1.5 hour wait time. 2.5 hours later all they had accomplished is looking at our teeth.  When I talked to Stacy Bedolla about his bill and the discrepancies, that I found out by looking at our dental insurance coverage, that Stacy had overcharged us for services which was covered under our insurance by almost $1500.00. We cancelled the subsequent appointments, because of how horrible the service was. The bays are all open with no privacy. The doctor was talking to another patient using the computer in my stall and telling all of the other patient's private information and dental issues to 8 different patients. After this we received two calls each day for collections on services that were never rendered and under a contract that was never signed. I called Western Dental on 3 occasions to get them to correct the collections, as we did not owe them anything. He called again on 10/31/2014 and talked to Cynthia. He paid $49.99 to pay for the fluoride which wasn't covered under our dental plan, which he hadn't agree to have done anyway. The calls continued twice a day with the letters that we owed them money for services they had never rendered. I contacted Leslie on 11/4/2014 to try and get the account reflected that we didn't owe them anything. The calls and the mail continued despite 3 more phone calls to request that they close the account, because it had paid in full and the other services never rendered. Magically they lost all of our information about our calls. He spoke to Jessica on 11/14/14, she stated she could not talk to him about the account, which was wrong, because it was all about him. I called on 11/17/2014 and talked to Chris which then transferred me to Victor which then transferred me to Connie (Supervisor) after a 30 minute hold time, and she said the account was closed and she would send me out a 0 balance letter. We will see if they followed through. DON'T GO HERE UNLESS YOU HAVE NO OTHER OPTIONS!!! Please understand I have never written a bad report about anybody on the internet, but their business warrants 100 bad reviews. We are now going to Fresno with another Dental Company.<//Review>
